src/app/store/cubicacion/cubicacion.actions.ts

agenciaSelected
Default value : createAction( '[CUBICACION] agenciaSelected ', props<{ agenciaSelected: AgenciaContrato }>() )
clonarCubicacion
Default value : createAction( '[CUBICACION] clonarCubicacion ', props<{ request: RequestCreateCubicacion }>() )
clonarCubicacionError
Default value : createAction( '[CUBICACION] clonarCubicacion Error', props<{ error: any }>() )
clonarCubicacionSuccess
Default value : createAction( '[CUBICACION] clonarCubicacion Success', props<{ response: Response<{ cubicacion_id: number }> }>() )
contratoSelected
Default value : createAction( '[CUBICACION] contratoSelected ', props<{ contratoUserSelected: ContratosUser }>() )
createCubicacion
Default value : createAction( '[CUBICACION] createCubicacion ', props<{ request: RequestCreateCubicacion }>() )

Featurekey
Type : string
Default value : 'auth'
initialState
Type : StateAuth
Default value : { sessionData: null, isLoggin: false, showMenuDetalleOT: false, }
reducerAuth
Default value : createReducer( initialState, on(authActions.loginSuccess, (state, { response }) => ({ ...state, sessionData: response.data, })), on(authActions.refreshLogin, (state, { proxy_id, nombre_perfil, rol }) => ({ ...state, sessionData: { ...state.sessionData, perfil_proxy_id: proxy_id, nombre_perfil_select: nombre_perfil, rol, }, })), on(authActions.refreshLoginSuccess, (state, { response }) => ({ ...state, sessionData: { ...state.sessionData, token: response.data.token, }, })), on( authActions.getPermisosPerfilUsuario4LoginSuccess, (state, { response }) => ({ ...state, sessionData: { ...state.sessionData, permisos: response.data.permisos, }, isLoggin: true, }) ), on(authActions.resetPerfil, (state, {}) => ({ ...state, sessionData: { ...state.sessionData, permisos: [], }, isLoggin: false, })), on(authActions.ClearSession, (state, {}) => initialState), on(authActions.showMenuDetalleOT, (state, { status }) => ({ ...state, showMenuDetalleOT: status, })) )
